</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">症状：</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">波动性渐进性听力下降</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">耳鸣</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">和耳涨满</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">感</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:22pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">辅助检查：</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">感</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">音性听力下降</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">耳蜗电图：</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">-SP</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">增大</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">冷热试验：患耳弱</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">甘油试验</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：阳性</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">Hennebert</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">征</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：膨大球囊接触镫骨，外耳道压力变化可引起眼震眩晕</span></p></td><td style="width:261.7pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">药物治疗和手术治疗</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold">手术：</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">听力保存：包括前庭功能是否保存两个手术</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">前庭功能保存：内淋巴分流；内淋巴减压；</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">交感神经节封闭；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="width:21pt; display:inline-block">&#xa0;</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">不保存：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">化学药物前庭破坏</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（最有效）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；膜迷路破坏</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；前庭神经切除术。</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">听力不保存：迷路切除术。</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">&#xa0;</span></p></td><td style="width:181.55pt; border-top:0.75pt solid #7f7f7f; border-bottom:0.75pt solid #7f7f7f; padding-right:5.4pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">症状：体位改变</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">引起</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">的发作性眩晕</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">1min</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">内）</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">辅助检查：</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌窦炎：晨起不痛，上午轻，午后重</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:22pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Wingdings"></span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">额窦炎：晨起开始痛，午后消失，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">周期出现</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:22pt; margin-bottom:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">前组筛窦炎：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">内</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">眦</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌窦穿刺：急性上颌窦炎无并发症</span></p></td><td style="width:181.55pt; padding-right:5.4pt; padding-left:5.4pt; vertical-align:top"><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">如果感染是发生在皮肤，或者容易引流，具有自净作用的粘膜，是不必全身用抗生素的；但是如果感染发生在不易引流、清洁，或者血</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">流丰富</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">地方，是要考虑全身使用抗生素的。</span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="width:59.85pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">好发于</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">纤毛上皮和鳞状上皮的移行部位</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="width:59.85pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">声门型最多（转移少，预后好）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">声</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">门上次之</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">耳后动脉</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">茎乳动脉：鼓室后部和乳突；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽升动脉</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼓室下动脉：鼓室下部和鼓室肌肉；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈内动脉</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼓室支：鼓室前壁。</span></p><ol start="15" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:18pt; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">鼻</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">内孔</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（鼻阈）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">中鼻甲基板：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">前后组筛窦的分界</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻道的开口：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">下鼻道：鼻泪管；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">中鼻道：前组筛窦、上颌窦和额窦开口；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">c)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上鼻道：蝶筛隐窝：蝶窦的开口。</span></p><ol start="4" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">总鼻道：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">中鼻甲以下</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。【中鼻甲以上和鼻中隔之间为</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">嗅裂（嗅沟）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">】</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻腔和鼻中隔的血管和神经：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">血管</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span></p><ol type="i" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈内动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">眼动脉：</span><ol type="1" style="margin-right:0pt; margin-left:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">筛前动脉：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻腔外侧壁和鼻中隔前上部；</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">筛后动脉：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻腔外侧壁和鼻中隔后上部；</span></li></ol></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈外动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">蝶腭动脉；</span><ol type="1" style="margin-right:0pt; margin-left:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻后外侧动脉：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻腔外侧壁后部、下部和鼻腔底；</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻后中隔动脉：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻中隔后部、下部；【进一步分支为</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">鼻腭动脉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">】</span></li></ol></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈外动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">眶下动脉：鼻腔外侧壁前段；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈外动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭大动脉：鼻中隔下部；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈外动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">面动脉</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上唇动脉：</span><span>Little Area</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻中隔前下部：</span><span>Little Area</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">、克氏静脉丛；鼻腔后侧：吴氏静脉丛（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">老年人好出血区</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）；</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">神经：</span></p><ol type="i" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">三叉神经</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">眼神经：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">筛前</span><span>/</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">后神经，区域同同名动脉；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">三叉神经</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上颌神经：</span><ol type="1" style="margin-right:0pt; margin-left:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">蝶</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">神经：鼻后上外侧支（外侧壁）和鼻后上内侧支（鼻中隔）；</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻腭神经：鼻中隔；</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">眶下神经：鼻前庭、上颌窦。</span></li></ol></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">翼管神经：</span><ol type="1" style="margin-right:0pt; margin-left:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">交感：来自岩深神经</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（颈动脉交感丛）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; padding-left:9.03pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">副交感：来自岩浅大神经（来自</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">面神经</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）。</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">岩浅小神经来自舌咽神经，支配腮腺腺体分泌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li></ol></li></ol><ol start="6" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">神经总结：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岩浅大神经来自面神经，支配腺体分泌；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岩浅小神经来自舌咽神经，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">是</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">鼓室神经的终末支</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">支配腮腺分泌；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">c)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼓索神经来自</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">面神经，入舌神经管理前</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">2/3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">味觉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；【舌后</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">1/3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">为舌咽神经的舌支】</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><ol start="7" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻窦淋巴</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽后淋巴结</span><span>→</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">颈深上淋巴</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">结</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li></ol><h2 style="margin-top:13pt; margin-bottom:13pt; text-align:justify; page-break-inside:avoid; page-break-after:avoid; line-height:173%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:16pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽科学</span></h2><ol type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽的分部：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻咽：</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">1</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">、</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">2</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">之前；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">口咽：</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">2</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">、</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">之前</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">c)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉咽：</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">下</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">部</span><span style="font-family:Cambria">~C</span><span style="font-family:Cambria; font-size:7pt; vertical-align:sub">6</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">上部</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">会厌上缘</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">到</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">环状软骨下缘</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><ol start="2" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腺样体：</span><span>6~7</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岁最显著，</span><span>10</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岁后逐步退化。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">鼻咽的咽隐窝后外方是腮腺后间隙</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：走行</span><span>9~12</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">脑神经、颈内静脉、颈内动脉和</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">颈交感神经节</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽鼓管相关肌肉：腭帆张肌和腭帆提肌：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭帆张肌：起自蝶骨角</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">棘</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">至</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">翼</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">突根部之间的骨面、蝶骨舟状窝、咽鼓管软骨外侧板和咽鼓管膜板等处的肌肉。</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'"> </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">肌纤维向前下方</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">移形成</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">小腱，绕过翼突钩，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">分散止</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">于腭腱膜。具有</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">紧张腭肌，扩大咽鼓管</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">的作用</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭帆提肌：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">起自颞骨岩部基底面和颈动脉管外口前面的肌肉，肌纤维行向前下方入咽，止于腭腱膜。具有</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">提升腭帆，开大咽鼓管咽口</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">的作用。</span></p><ol start="5" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭咽弓后方有</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">纵行条索</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">淋巴组织</span><span>——</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽侧索。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">扁桃体表面向内凹陷构成</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">扁桃体隐窝</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">扁桃体在</span><span>3~5</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岁显著增大（注意不是咽扁桃体！）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">扁桃体的动脉和神经：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">动脉：主要是</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">面动脉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">的扁桃体支；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">神经：上端来自</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">蝶</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">腭</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">神经节</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">的</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">腭</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">后</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">和</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">腭</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">中神经</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；下端为舌咽神经的</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">扁桃体支</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。【</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">舌咽神经和面神经在颌面部的腺体、运动、感觉是互补的</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，原因在于起源核团的互补性】</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><ol start="9" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">咽部没有粘膜下组织</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，粘膜和纤维紧密相连。</span></li><li style="margin-left:18pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽壁的肌层包括</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽缩肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">组：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上中下，依次收缩助吞咽</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">提肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">组：茎突咽肌、咽鼓管咽肌、腭咽肌（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">咽上的</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">结构和咽相连，提起咽</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）：</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">c)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭帆肌组</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">以软腭为核心，除了</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">迷走神经支配腭帆张肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，其他均由</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">上颌神经支配</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span></p><ol type="i" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭帆张肌：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">蝶骨翼突</span><span>~</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">软腭（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">开大咽鼓管</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭帆提肌：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">岩尖</span><span>~</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">悬雍垂（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">缩小咽鼓管</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）；</span></li><li style="margin-left:49pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:17pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">腭舌肌、腭咽肌、悬雍垂肌。</span></li></ol><ol start="11" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:18pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽后间隙</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">【</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">颈深筋膜中层到椎前筋膜</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">】</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">两侧咽后间隙不相同，咽后间隙有</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">前后组淋巴结</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></li><li style="margin-left:18pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">咽旁间隙</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">【</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">咽侧壁、翼内肌、椎前筋膜</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">之间的间隙】</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">茎突分为前后两区：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">前部：内含</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">茎突咽肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">、</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">茎突舌肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">上方和咽隐窝关系密切</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">后部：颈动脉鞘和周围神经。</span></p><ol start="13" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:18pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-family:Cambria; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">鼻咽：咽后淋巴结、颈深上淋巴结和胸锁乳突肌后缘淋巴结；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">口咽：下颌角淋巴结、颈深中淋巴结；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">c)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉咽：颈深中淋巴结</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">d)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">舌根、会厌谷：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">锥前淋巴结</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:13pt; margin-bottom:13pt; text-align:justify; page-break-inside:avoid; page-break-after:avoid; line-height:173%; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:16pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">科学</span></h2><ol type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">喉部</span><span style="font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">9</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">软骨</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：环状、甲状、会厌；</span><span>2×</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">杓</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">状、</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">楔</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">状、小角）。</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">【</span><span style="font-weight:bold; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">甲状舌骨膜：喉上神经内支</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">和喉上动脉穿过。</span></li><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">弹性膜：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">方形膜</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（阻挡声门上癌扩展）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上缘：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">杓</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">会厌韧带；下缘：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">室韧带</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">弹性圆锥</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（阻挡声带癌扩展）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">上缘：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">声韧带</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；前方：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">环甲膜</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><ol start="4" type="1" style="margin:0pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉内肌【</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">起止点在喉内</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">】</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：</span></li></ol><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">a)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">环杓后肌：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">唯一的外展肌，声门开大</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">环杓侧肌和</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">杓</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">肌：</span></p><ol type="i" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:49pt; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">【喉返神经前支支配了</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">杓肌和环杓后肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">，其余都是后支支配】</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">环甲肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">（</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">喉上神经</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">）</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">：增加声带张力；</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">【</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">喉上神经还支配咽下缩肌</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">】</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">d)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">甲杓肌：降低声带张力，关闭声门；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">杓</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">会厌肌：关闭喉；甲状会厌肌：打开喉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">。</span></p><ol start="7" type="1" style="margin:0pt; padding-left:0pt"><li style="margin-left:12.97pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">喉</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">粘膜大多为假复层纤毛柱状上皮；</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; padding-left:5.03pt; font-family:Cambria; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:'宋体'">声门：</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">前</span><span style="font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">2/3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">为膜间部，后</span><span style="font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">1/3</span><span style="font-family:'宋体'; </span><span style="font-family:'宋体'">声门上：颈深下；</span></p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-left:44pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:-22pt; text-align:justify; widows:0; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt"><span style="font-family:Cambria">b)</span><span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman'">&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;
